if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'c532904d2b07a67a1f792e62ba9e3411f6cb2099') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'c532904d2b07a67a1f792e62ba9e3411f6cb2099') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'bc75a374c983f9bde5874432f56158ed5a3d8de3') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'c532904d2b07a67a1f792e62ba9e3411f6cb2099') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/config_values.txt');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') != 'ffc43f76594ac7c8713b891edd209b5df043ca0c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/config_values.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/config_values.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'ffc43f76594ac7c8713b891edd209b5df043ca0c') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'f9646fb1fd2da097d682f8a55b49e8fc52ee810b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/config_values.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/config_values.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/config_values.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/config_values.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'ffc43f76594ac7c8713b891edd209b5df043ca0c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != 'ce04ff1934b25fbc244f34c81f915ca3f5a6c374') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'ce04ff1934b25fbc244f34c81f915ca3f5a6c374') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'ee89a26f64292e459a0bee259e9d71c6b5ec4719') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'ce04ff1934b25fbc244f34c81f915ca3f5a6c374') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'ced177958476c265b4fdc80dfdecfec0cd24cb70') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'ced177958476c265b4fdc80dfdecfec0cd24cb70') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '4ac584adf44c2c01f43fe86d93045017cc4ff3b3') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'ced177958476c265b4fdc80dfdecfec0cd24cb70') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html') != 'aab5ce9628bcc106ee12ab3174242d7973fb1e73') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html') !== 'aab5ce9628bcc106ee12ab3174242d7973fb1e73') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html') !== 'b5fd8bb1560d5ac2d58bd892a358943e77f3550d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html') !== 'aab5ce9628bcc106ee12ab3174242d7973fb1e73') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') != '2fa734f9498653be90a4a44db683b1ab1a2faf2e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== '2fa734f9498653be90a4a44db683b1ab1a2faf2e') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== '8c35d70e9579a400973f0a525ec806eafd90038d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== '2fa734f9498653be90a4a44db683b1ab1a2faf2e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') != '50b80d7604423ad03ffef2bd9e1d7ef400028b49') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/includes/setup_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== '50b80d7604423ad03ffef2bd9e1d7ef400028b49') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== '2c48c9cc0815be4f93dbd525f9aa4d6a851b2587') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/includes/setup_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/includes/setup_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/includes/setup_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/includes/setup_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== '50b80d7604423ad03ffef2bd9e1d7ef400028b49') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/index.php');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/index.php') != '4afef6c4d4f54b6c89224f96f7a3a8b80a6b1896') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '4afef6c4d4f54b6c89224f96f7a3a8b80a6b1896') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '877954973d98fc5f4d5c40bb4f9edac8c6931dff') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '4afef6c4d4f54b6c89224f96f7a3a8b80a6b1896') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 974\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 974') err('Could not write to .version.php!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3
